<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:писательство.html>писа́тельство</a> (27936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писатель.html>писа́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писательство.html>писа́тельство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pisátelʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писательство.html>писа́тельства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писательство.html>писа́тельства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писательство.html>писа́тельств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>authorship <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the activity or craft of a writer</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***писать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писать</a> (223)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">писати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to write; to paint</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pisati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*peyḱ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">paint</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">picture</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:написать.html>написа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to write</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to paint (a painting)</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">pissen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">pissier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*pissiō</i>, of echoic origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>пи́сать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">písatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пописать.html>попи́сать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to urinate, to pee, to piss</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be hot for, to be sexually attracted to</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писать</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́ры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:диктофон.html>диктофо́н</a>. </span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:писаться.html>пи́саться</a> (6713)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писаться.html>писа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pisátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">написа́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span> to spell, to be spelt; to be spelled
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:писаться.html>пи́шется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>píšetsja</b> éto slóvo?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">how do you spell this word?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писаться.html>пи́саться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">písatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>пи́сать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">písatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>to urinate (accidentally), to pee, to piss, to wet one's bed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:детство.html>де́тстве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:писаться.html>пи́сался</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V détstve on částo <b>písalsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He often wet his bed when he was little.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писе́ц</a> (17687)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to write</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ц</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-éc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писе́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">piséc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писцы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писцо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>copyist, penman, scribe, scrivener, writer</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пи́счий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">písčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Euphemistic modification of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пизде́ц</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pizdéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>пи́сать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">písatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to piss</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писе́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">piséc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писцы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писцо́в</a></b>)

***пискнувший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пискнувший.html>пи́скнувший</a> (12793)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистолет</a> (1273)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pistolet</i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">píšťala</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whistle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*piščalь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*piskati, *piščati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeak, whistle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*pīṣk-</i>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищаль.html>пища́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">piščálʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистоле́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pistolét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистоле́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистоле́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистоле́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pistol, handgun</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пистолетик.html>пистоле́тик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pistoletik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pisьmo</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">писмѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pismę</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">letter <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the alphabet</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; writing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (genitive <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">писмене</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pismene</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>

***питание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́ние</a> (2762)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pitánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>food, nutrition, alimentation</li>
<li>power (<i>electrical supply</i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еда.html>еда́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jedá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кормление.html>кормле́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kormlénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́ща</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">píšča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подко́рмка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podkórmka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:питательный.html>пита́тельный</a> (12976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питательный.html>пита́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pitátelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>nourishing, nutritious</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> feeding, feed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nutrient
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питательный.html>пита́тельная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:среда.html>среда́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátelʹnaja</b> sredá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nutrient medium</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питательный.html>пита́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:раствор.html>раство́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátelʹnyj</b> rastvór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nutrient solution</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питательный.html>пита́тельные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещество.html>вещества́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátelʹnyje</b> veščestvá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nutrients</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***питать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a> (7571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pitátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напитать.html>напита́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to feed, to nourish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́го</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátʹ</b> bolʹnóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feed a patient</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to supply
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:электроэнергия.html>электроэне́ргией</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátʹ</b> górod elektroenɛ́rgijej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to supply a city with electricity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátʹ</b> boj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feed the battle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to feel, to experience <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a prolonged or constant manner</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátʹ</b> čúvstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to nourish/entertain a feeling</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нежный.html>не́жные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátʹ</b> néžnyje čúvstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a tender affection</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:симпатия.html>симпа́тию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátʹ</b> simpátiju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feel sympathy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвращение.html>отвраще́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátʹ</b> otvraščénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have aversion; loathe</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitátʹ</b> nadéždu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cherish/nourish the hope</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a> (587)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">piti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*piti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выпить.html>вы́пить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попить.html>попи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drink
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> (<i>idiom</i>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak pítʹ datʹ (<i>idiom</i>)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for sure, as sure as eggs are eggs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рькую</a> (<i>idiom</i>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitʹ</b> górʹkuju (<i>idiom</i>)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drink hard</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Dated usage places the stress on <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> when negated in the past tense, hence <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пил</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пи́ло</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пили</a></span> (but always <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пила́</a></span>). This usage is no longer current.</li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питье.html>питьё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitʹjó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питьевой.html>питьево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pitʹjevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drinking; potable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питьевой.html>питьева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вода́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitʹjevája</b> vodá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>drinking/potable</b> water</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:питьевой.html>питьево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фонтанчик.html>фонта́нчик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pitʹjevój</b> fontánčik</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>drinking</b> fountain</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пихать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пихать.html>пиха́ть</a> (23744)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пихати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pixati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пихать.html>пиха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pixátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пихнуть.html>пихну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to push, to shove, to elbow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shove <i>(into)</i></li></ol>

***пихнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пихнуть.html>пихну́ть</a> (20049)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пихать.html>пиха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pixátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пихнуть.html>пихну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pixnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пихать.html>пиха́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to push, to shove, to elbow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shove <i>(into)</i></li></ol>
